---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, patient_name, patient_dob
- medication table with columns:
  medication_id, medication_name, patient_id
- medication_admin table with columns:
  medication_admin_id, medication_id, patient_id, admin_date, dose, dose_unit

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with a dose greater than 10mg.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use medication_admin as the main table
- JOIN patient on patient_id
- JOIN medication on medication_id
- WHERE medication_admin.dose > 10
- ORDER BY patient.patient_name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_name,
  p.patient_dob,
  m.medication_name,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose,
  ma.dose_unit
FROM 
  medication_admin ma
  JOIN patient p ON ma.patient_id = p.patient_id
  JOIN medication m ON ma.medication_id = m.medication_id
WHERE 
  ma.dose > 10
ORDER BY 
  p.patient_name ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10027445
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

```sql
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10020740
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```


---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10020740
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10038999
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10039708
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, name, age, gender
- medication table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, start_date, end_date
- medication_admin table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, admin_date, dose

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with medication_id = 12345, including the medication start and end dates, and the medication administration dates.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patient as the main table
- LEFT JOIN medication ON patient_id
- LEFT JOIN medication_admin ON patient_id
- WHERE medication.medication_id = 12345
- ORDER BY patient.name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.name,
  p.age,
  p.gender,
  m.start_date,
  m.end_date,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose
FROM 
  patient p
  LEFT JOIN medication m ON p.patient_id = m.patient_id
  LEFT JOIN medication_admin ma ON p.patient_id = ma.patient_id
WHERE 
  m.medication_id = 12345
ORDER BY 
  p.name ASC;
```

The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type

```sql

  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,

  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10019385
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, name, age, gender
- medication table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, start_date, end_date
- medication_admin table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, admin_date, dose

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with medication_id = 12345, including the medication start date and end date.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patient as the main table
- LEFT JOIN medication ON patient_id
- LEFT JOIN medication_admin ON patient_id
- WHERE medication.medication_id = 12345
- ORDER BY patient.name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.name,
  p.age,
  p.gender,
  m.start_date,
  m.end_date,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose
FROM 
  patient p
  LEFT JOIN medication m ON p.patient_id = m.patient_id
  LEFT JOIN medication_admin ma ON p.patient_id = ma.patient_id
WHERE 
  m.medication_id = 12345
ORDER BY 
  p.name ASC;
```

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10022041
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,

  ie.endtime,

  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE

ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

- d_items table with columns:

Task:
Get all ingredient events for subject_id = 10009035, including the medication label from d_items.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10009035
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,

  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10009035
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

- SELECT only
- Use patient as the main table

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.name,
  p.age,
  p.gender,
  m.start_date,

  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose

  LEFT JOIN medication_admin ma ON p.patient_id = ma.patient_id
WHERE

ORDER BY
```

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, name, age, gender
- medication table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, start_date, end_date
- medication_admin table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, admin_date, dose

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with medication_id = 12345, including the medication start date and end date.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patient as the main table
- LEFT JOIN medication ON patient_id
- LEFT JOIN medication_admin ON patient_id
- WHERE medication.medication_id = 12345
- ORDER BY patient.name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.name,
  p.age,
  p.gender,
  m.start_date,
  m.end_date,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose
FROM 
  patient p
  LEFT JOIN medication m ON p.patient_id = m.patient_id
  LEFT JOIN medication_admin ma ON p.patient_id = ma.patient_id
WHERE 
  m.medication_id = 12345
ORDER BY 
  p.name ASC;
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10038081
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
```
```sql
  ie.subject_id = 10011398
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
```
```sql
  ie.subject_id = 10004457
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

- ingredientevents table with columns:
  subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom,

- d_items table with columns:
  itemid, label

Task:
Get all ingredient events for subject_id = 10013049, including the medication label from d_items.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10013049
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10013049
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10013049
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- ingredientevents table with columns:
  subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom,
  rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription
- d_items table with columns:
  itemid, label

Task:
Get all ingredient events for subject_id = 10029484, including the medication label from d_items.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10029484
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10029484
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```


---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10029484
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

- ingredientevents table with columns:
  subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom,
  rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription
- d_items table with columns:
  itemid, label

Task:
Get all ingredient events for subject_id = 10004720, including the medication label from d_items.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10004720
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10004720
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, patient_name, patient_dob
- medication table with columns:
  medication_id, medication_name, patient_id
- medication_admin table with columns:
  medication_admin_id, medication_id, patient_id, admin_date, dose, dose_unit

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with a dose greater than 10mg.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use medication_admin as the main table
- JOIN patient on patient_id
- JOIN medication on medication_id
- WHERE medication_admin.dose > 10
- ORDER BY patient.patient_name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_name,
  p.patient_dob,
  m.medication_name,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose,
  ma.dose_unit
FROM 
  medication_admin ma
  JOIN patient p ON ma.patient_id = p.patient_id
  JOIN medication m ON ma.medication_id = m.medication_id
WHERE 
  ma.dose > 10
ORDER BY 
  p.patient_name ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
```
```sql
  ie.subject_id = 10019917
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10010471
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

- d_items table with columns:
  itemid, label

Task:
Get all ingredient events for subject_id = 10007818, including the medication label from d_items.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use ingredientevents as the main table
- LEFT JOIN d_items ON itemid
- WHERE ingredientevents.subject_id = 10007818
- ORDER BY starttime ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python

RAW SQL OUTPUT:
code

```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10007818
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
```
```sql
  ie.subject_id = 10019568
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, patient_name, patient_dob
- medication table with columns:
  medication_id, medication_name, patient_id
- medication_admin table with columns:
  medication_admin_id, medication_id, patient_id, admin_date, dose, dose_unit

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with a dose greater than 10mg.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use medication_admin as the main table
- JOIN patient on patient_id
- JOIN medication on medication_id
- WHERE medication_admin.dose > 10
- ORDER BY patient.patient_name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_name,
  p.patient_dob,
  m.medication_name,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose,
  ma.dose_unit
FROM 
  medication_admin ma
  JOIN patient p ON ma.patient_id = p.patient_id
  JOIN medication m ON ma.medication_id = m.medication_id
WHERE 
  ma.dose > 10
ORDER BY 
  p.patient_name ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10019003
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patients table with columns:
  patient_id, patient_name, patient_dob
- diagnoses table with columns:
  patient_id, icd9_code, icd9_description, start_date, end_date
- procedures table with columns:
  patient_id, procedure_id, procedure_name, start_date, end_date

Task:
Get all patients with at least one diagnosis and one procedure, including patient name, date of birth, diagnosis ICD-9 code, procedure ID, and procedure name.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patients as the main table
- INNER JOIN diagnoses ON patient_id
- INNER JOIN procedures ON patient_id
- WHERE diagnoses.patient_id = patients.patient_id AND procedures.patient_id = patients.patient_id
- GROUP BY patients.patient_id
- HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT diagnoses.icd9_code) > 0 AND COUNT(DISTINCT procedures.procedure_id) > 0
- ORDER BY patients.patient_name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.patient_name,
  p.patient_dob,
  d.icd9_code,
  pr.procedure_id,
  pr.procedure_name
FROM 
  patients p
  INNER JOIN diagnoses d ON p.patient_id = d.patient_id
  INNER JOIN procedures pr ON p.patient_id = pr.patient_id
WHERE 
  d.patient_id = p.patient_id AND pr.patient_id = p.patient_id
GROUP BY 
  p.patient_id
HAVING 
  COUNT(DISTINCT d.icd9_code) > 0 AND COUNT(DISTINCT pr.procedure_id) > 0
ORDER BY 
  p.patient_name ASC;
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10007795
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patient table with columns:
  patient_id, name, age, gender
- medication table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, start_date, end_date
- medication_admin table with columns:
  patient_id, medication_id, admin_date, dose

Task:
Get all patients who have taken medication with medication_id = 12345, including the medication start date and end date.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patient as the main table
- LEFT JOIN medication ON patient_id
- LEFT JOIN medication_admin ON patient_id
- WHERE medication.medication_id = 12345
- ORDER BY patient.name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.name,
  p.age,
  p.gender,
  m.start_date,
  m.end_date,
  ma.admin_date,
  ma.dose
FROM 
  patient p
  LEFT JOIN medication m ON p.patient_id = m.patient_id
  LEFT JOIN medication_admin ma ON p.patient_id = ma.patient_id
WHERE 
  m.medication_id = 12345
ORDER BY 
  p.name ASC;
```

---

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10018328
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

### Step 5: Review and refine the query
The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.

---

You are a clinical SQL assistant.

Write ONE SQLite query using:
- patients table with columns:
  patient_id, patient_name, patient_dob
- diagnoses table with columns:
  patient_id, icd9_code, icd9_description, start_date, end_date
- procedures table with columns:
  patient_id, procedure_id, procedure_name, start_date, end_date

Task:
Get all patients with at least one diagnosis and one procedure, including patient name, date of birth, diagnosis ICD-9 code, procedure ID, and procedure name.

Rules:
- SELECT only
- Use patients as the main table
- INNER JOIN diagnoses ON patient_id
- INNER JOIN procedures ON patient_id
- WHERE diagnoses.patient_id = patients.patient_id AND procedures.patient_id = patients.patient_id
- GROUP BY patients.patient_id
- HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT diagnoses.icd9_code) > 0 AND COUNT(DISTINCT procedures.procedure_id) > 0
- ORDER BY patients.patient_name ASC
- Return SQL only
- Do not explain anything
- Do not return Python code

```sql
SELECT 
  p.patient_id,
  p.patient_name,
  p.patient_dob,
  d.icd9_code,
  pr.procedure_id,
  pr.procedure_name
FROM 
  patients p
  INNER JOIN diagnoses d ON p.patient_id = d.patient_id
  INNER JOIN procedures pr ON p.patient_id = pr.patient_id
WHERE 
  d.patient_id = p.patient_id AND pr.patient_id = p.patient_id
GROUP BY 
  p.patient_id
HAVING 
  COUNT(DISTINCT d.icd9_code) > 0 AND COUNT(DISTINCT pr.procedure_id) > 0
ORDER BY 
  p.patient_name ASC;
```

### Step 1: Define the problem and the goal
The goal is to write a SQLite query that retrieves all ingredient events for a specific subject_id from the ingredientevents table, along with the medication label from the d_items table.

### Step 2: Identify the required tables and columns
The required tables are ingredientevents and d_items. The required columns are subject_id, hadm_id, stay_id, itemid, starttime, endtime, amount, amountuom, rate, rateuom, originalrate, statusdescription from ingredientevents, and label from d_items.

### Step 3: Determine the join type
Since we need to retrieve the medication label from d_items for each ingredient event in ingredientevents, we will use a LEFT JOIN.

### Step 4: Write the query
```sql
SELECT 
  ie.subject_id,
  ie.hadm_id,
  ie.stay_id,
  ie.itemid,
  ie.starttime,
  ie.endtime,
  ie.amount,
  ie.amountuom,
  ie.rate,
  ie.rateuom,
  ie.originalrate,
  ie.statusdescription,
  di.label
FROM 
  ingredientevents ie
  LEFT JOIN d_items di ON ie.itemid = di.itemid
WHERE 
  ie.subject_id = 10020640
ORDER BY 
  ie.starttime ASC;
```

The query is complete and meets all the requirements. No further refinement is needed.
